    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Zion's
<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">'2010 Annual Meeting'</font>
took place on Monday, June 14, 2010, in Caesarea, Israel. Present at the meeting
were stockholders who had travelled to Israel from as far away as Finland and
California, USA; I believe that everyone attending enjoyed the very positive
spirit of the meeting.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><img src="pic2.jpg" alt=""></font></div>

</font>(R)</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">One
V.I.P. guest present at the meeting was Victor Carrillo (pictured above), the
Chairman of the Railroad Commission of Texas. The Railroad Commission is the
primary regulator of the oil and gas industry in Texas and it was a great honor
for Zion to have Chairman Carrillo present at our meeting.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
business formalities were duly carried out and the resolutions were successfully
carried. After the formal part of the meeting, I gave my report of Zion's
activities during the prior twelve months and then Zion's President and Chief
Operating Officer, Bill Ottaviani, gave his report.</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Summit will take place in Washington, D.C. during July 20th to 22nd and the
banquet will take place on Wednesday evening, July 21, 2010. Pastor John Hagee
and Israel&#8217;s Ambassador to the U.S., Michael Oren, are scheduled to speak at the
banquet.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">It is
expected that John Brown, Zion&#8217;s Founder and Chairman, will be interviewed by
Pastor John Hagee during the Summit and that the interview will be broadcast on
the Daystar Television Network during the &#8220;Night to Honor Israel&#8221;. In addition,
CUFI will broadcast a video about Zion at the banquet&#8217;s pre-event, and the
banquet&#8217;s proceedings will be telecast by live-feed over the Daystar Television
network. If you want to read the press release, please click here.</font></div>

OFFERING</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The

5:00 p.m. EDT on June 30, 2010, so if you want to subscribe but have not yet

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Under the
rights offering (see www.zionoil.com/investor-center) Zion stockholders, at the
close of business on May 6, 2010, were issued, at no charge, the
following:</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">ONE
subscription right for every TWO shares of stock owned (as of the close of
business on May 6, 2010).</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Each
subscription right entitles the holder to purchase one share of Zion stock at a
price of $5.00, irrespective of the market price at the time of
purchase.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
subscription rights may be exercised at any time prior to the end of June 2010.
However, after 5:00 pm EDT on June 30, 2010, unexercised subscriptions rights
will expire with no residual value.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Please
note that if you want to exercise your rights and you hold your stock in a
brokerage account, then you will need to contact your broker to determine when
and how you can exercise your rights, as each individual brokerage firm has
their own timeline and procedures for processing subscriptions.</font></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
detailed in the press release, we plan to use the proceeds from the rights
offering: (a) to purchase a 51% interest in a new yet to be established company
(Zion Drilling, Inc. that will own a 2,000 horsepower drilling rig), (b) to
drill further 'deep' exploration wells on Zion's licenses in Israel (in
continuation of Zion's oil and gas exploration efforts) and (c) for general
corporate purposes.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">....................................................</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">With
regard to 'Operations', we are now preparing for the next well, as you can
read.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma'anit-Joseph #3 Well (M-J
#3)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We
continue moving forward through the many permitting requirements for the M-J #3
well and are securing all the necessary services and equipment to ensure an &#8220;on
time&#8221; spud date.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">When the
permitting process for this well began, we estimated a 5-month time frame would
be needed to secure the necessary permits before well site construction could
begin.&#160;&#160;As it is turning out, we need every bit of this time to
navigate through the complex permitting process for a new well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We
currently plan to begin well site construction in early July 2010. The
construction of the concrete platform will take approximately four
weeks.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On the
equipment and services procurement front, we are making steady
progress.&#160;&#160;All the equipment needed on site by our planned spud date
has been ordered and delivery confirmations have been received.&#160;&#160;This
first large order of equipment is primarily for well casing and wellhead
equipment &#8211; equipment that often requires a long delivery lead
time.&#160;&#160;We are expecting the first shipment of this equipment within
the next few weeks.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Additionally,
most of the major services we require for drilling have already been awarded
through our bidding process and service contracts are in the process of being
prepared.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All in
all, our work progress is steady and we remain on schedule for an <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">August 2010</font> spud date for the
M-J #3 well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">The Issachar-Zebulun Permit
Area</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On June
16, 2010, field acquisition of new 2-dimensional seismic in the Jordan River
Valley section of our Issachar-Zebulun permit area was successfully
concluded.&#160;&#160;Approximately 30 km of new seismic data was collected on
Zion&#8217;s behalf by the Geophysical Institute of Israel
(GII).&#160;&#160;Preliminary indications suggest that data quality is &#8216;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic">good</font>&#8217;.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>

    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This data
will soon be &#8220;processed&#8221; by a geophysical consultant in the United States into
usable graphic imagery that can then be &#8220;interpreted&#8221; by our geologists in their
investigation for future drilling prospects.&#160;&#160;The processing and
interpretation of this data is expected to be finalized by October
2010.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Elijah #3
Well</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As
previously noted, the Elijah #3 well was drilled to a depth of approximately
10,938 feet (3,334 meters) when the drill string became stuck within the Asher
Volcanics section of the hole. After recovering a significant portion of the
stuck drill pipe, progress in recovering the remainder of the pipe slowed and
the decision was made to temporarily suspend drilling operations pending further
analysis of the situation.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">We are
currently acquiring approximately 32 kilometers of additional field seismic data
that will help us to resolve certain questions regarding the geology of the area
surrounding this well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">GII began
field acquisition of this seismic on June 16, 2010, and have already finished
collecting data in one of three &#8220;lines&#8221; planned.&#160;&#160;Each of the three
planned seismic lines is geographically oriented in a different direction (for
example, one line may be east-west oriented and another may be north-south
oriented). This is to ensure that our geologists have sufficient areal coverage
of the geologic region to be investigated.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As with
the seismic data collected in the Issachar-Zebulun permit area, this data will
also need to be processed and subsequently interpreted.&#160;&#160;In this case,
however, we are not looking for new prospects but instead looking for greater
clarity in the geology that underlies our Elijah-3 well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Ma'anit-Rehoboth #2 Well
(M-R #2)</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">This well
is currently temporarily suspended for possible future use as an offset well to
the Ma'anit-Joseph #3 (M-J #3) well (see above) which is to be drilled a short
distance away.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">It is
important to note that we are drilling to the deep "Permian" structure in the
M-J #3 well; whereas the various intervals tested in the M-R #2 well consisted
of shallower and younger age rocks.&#160;&#160;As such, and despite the relative
proximity of these two wells, the results of the M-R #2 well tests are not
correlative to what we expect in the Permian of the M-J #3 well.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div id="PGBRK" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
      <div id="FTR">
        <div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left">

Rebalancing</font></font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The
Russell 3000 is a value weighted index that measures performance of the top
3,000 stocks of the investable U.S. equity market. Zion was placed on the index
as of June 26, 2009. In June of every year, the index is
reconstituted,</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On
Friday, June 25, 2010, after the stock market close, the 2010 reconstitution of
the Russell Indexes will take place, and Zion may not be part of the 2010 index.
In connection with the reconstitution, NASDAQ has advised us that, in the short
term, there may be increased trading volumes in Zion's stock trading and
volatility in Zion's stock price.</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As the
late great Benjamin Graham noted, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-STYLE: italic">'In the short term the market is a
voting machine, in the long term it is a weighing machine</font>".</font></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br></div>
    <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Zion's
management team are committed to building <font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">long term</font> value into
Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. and try to ignore fluctuations in Zion's stock price,
caused by events over which we have no control.&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div>
